## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time (t) and current population size (P). This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size through various feedback mechanisms such as density dependence, Allee effects, and environmental carrying capacity.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Malthusian exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Unlimited resources, growth rate proportional to population size'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreases logarithmically as population approaches carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Strong Allee effect with critical minimum population threshold'}
- {'name': 'Weak Allee effect', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate reduced at low densities but no critical threshold'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth'}
- {'name': 'Power-law density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Growth rate as a power function of population'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous form', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Recruitment with density-dependent limitation minus mortality'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent logistic', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * t * P', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with time-varying intrinsic rate'}
- {'name': 'Exponential decay growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate with exponential density regulation'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3', 'scenario': 'Polynomial expansion of density-dependent growth'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → multiplicative factor (1 - P/K) or (1 - c*P) reducing growth at high population
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) → multiplicative factor (P - c) introducing a lower critical threshold
- Logarithmic saturation in growth regulation → log(K/P) term as in Gompertz models
- Population growth rate proportional to P → dP_dt contains P as a multiplicative factor (extensive quantity scaling)
- Asymmetric growth curves → power transformation of density-dependent term (c*P)**n with n ≠ 1
- Time-explicit environmental forcing → additive or multiplicative terms involving t, sin(c*t), or exp(c*t)
- Mortality vs. reproduction separation → difference of two positive terms, each depending on P differently
- Self-limitation at high density → negative quadratic term -c*P**2 in the growth rate expression
